  - No, definitely not.

**Have you experienced any of the following psychological symptoms in the past month due to work-related stress?**

  - Difficulty concentrating or focusing
  - Other (please specify): __________________

**Do you feel that your job role and responsibilities align with your skills and abilities?**

  - I am not sure.
  - No, definitely not.

  - No, definitely not.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.

Generate me a questionnaire on Remote working experience with 10 questions

-------------------

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can generate a questionnaire about remote working experience. Here are 10 questions:

1. How would you describe your overall experience with remote work?
2. Which aspects of remote work do you find most challenging?
3. How do you feel about the communication and collaboration with your team when working remotely?
4. Do you feel that your productivity has been affected by remote work? If yes, in what way?
5. How do you feel about the technology and tools that you have been using for remote work?
6. How do you feel about the work-life balance when working remotely?
7. How do you feel about the flexibility of remote work?
8. How do you feel about the support from your organization when working remotely?
9. How do you feel about the possibility of continuing remote work in the future?
10. Is there anything else you would like to share about your remote work experience?

Please let me know if you would like me to convert this questionnaire into a specific format or if you have any other preferences for the questions.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Remote working experience with 10 questions

This JSON object represents a questionnaire with a single questionnaire containing 6 questions. Each question is represented as an object in the `_TF_QUESTIONS` array, and each answer is represented as an object in the `_TF_ANSWERS` array. The `TYPE_ID` property is used to determine the type of question, and the `DISPLAY_ORDER` property is used to determine the order in which the questions should be displayed. The `ANSWER` property is used to determine the content of each answer.

This JSON object represents a questionnaire for assessing career path clarity. The questionnaire consists of five questions, each with three possible answers. The questions are:

1. Do you feel that your current role aligns with your long-term career goals?
2. Have you ever received a promotion or a pay raise in your current company?
3. Do you have a clear understanding of the skills and competencies required to progress in your career?
4. Do you feel that your employer provides you with opportunities to learn and grow in your current role?
5. Do you have a clear understanding of the career paths available within your company?

Each question allows respondents to choose one of three possible answers: "Yes, completely", "Yes, somewhat", or "No, not at all". This questionnaire can help employers understand their employees' career aspirations and provide appropriate opportunities for growth.

This JSON object represents an employee motivation questionnaire with five questions. The first four questions are multiple choice questions with options "Yes", "No", and "Not sure". The last question is a text field for open-ended feedback. The "DISPLAY\_ORDER" property is used to order the questions. The "CODE" property is a unique identifier for each question, and "NAME" is the question content. The "TYPE\_ID" property is used to specify the type of question, and the "_TF\_ANSWERS" array contains the possible answers for multiple choice questions. The "ANSWER" property is the actual answer given by the respondent.

**Health and Safety Measures Questionnaire**

1. How often do you think about the health and safety measures in your workplace?
  - Never
  - Rarely
  - Occasionally
  - Most of the time
  - Always
2. Do you think the current health and safety measures in your workplace are sufficient?
  - Yes
  - No
3. Have you ever been involved in an accident at your workplace due to inadequate health and safety measures?
  - Yes
  - No
4. If you have been involved in an accident, how did it affect your work and life in general?
  - It had a significant negative impact on my work and life.
  - It had a moderate negative impact on my work and life.
  - It had a minor negative impact on my work and life.
  - It had no impact on my work and life.
5. How would you rate the communication about health and safety measures in your workplace?
  - Very poor
  - Poor
  - Average
  - Good
  - Very good
6. Have you ever received training on health and safety measures in your workplace?
  - Yes
  - No
7. If you have received training, how would you rate the training?
  - Very poor
  - Poor
  - Average
  - Good
  - Very good

The multiple-choice questions ask whether internal mobility opportunities are clearly communicated, accessible, a priority, and if adequate support and resources are provided. This JSON object represents a questionnaire with 7 questions. The first question asks about the length of time an employee has been with the company, and the second question asks if the employee has ever experienced the onboarding process. The third question asks if the employee thinks the onboarding process is long enough, and the fourth question asks if the onboarding process was effective in making the employee feel comfortable and welcome. The fifth question asks if the employee was provided with all necessary resources and materials during the onboarding process, and the sixth question asks if the onboarding process could be improved. The seventh question asks if the employee has any suggestions for improving the onboarding process. Each question has a unique code, name, type, and display order, and each question also has a list of possible answers. The answers are represented as a string, and the employee can select only one answer for questions with type 1, and multiple answers for questions with type 2. The employee can rate something for questions with type 3, and provide feedback for questions with type 4. The employee can reorder items for questions with type 5, and distribute weights across several items/options for questions with type 6. The employee can also clone questions from a template for questions with type 7, and answer a date or a date/time question with type 8.

This JSON object represents a questionnaire about work-life balance. It includes eight questions with the following details:

* Question code: unique identifier for the question
* Question name: display name of the question
* Question type: type of question (3 in this case means rating)
* Display order: order in which the question should be displayed
* Answers: a list of possible answers for the question

The answers are also unique for each question and represent the different options a respondent can choose from. In this case, the answers are represented as a simple string.
